  101 00000000         ;---------------------------------------------------------------
  102 00000000         ;UART0_BDH
  103 00000000         ;    0->  7:LIN break detect IE (disabled)

  105 00000000         ;    0->  5:Stop bit number select (1)
  106 00000000         ;00001->4-0:SBR[12:0] (UART0CLK / [9600 * (OSR + 1)]) 
  107 00000000         ;UART0CLK is MCGFLLCLK

  109 00000000         ;SBR ~=~ 48 MHz / (9600 * 16) = 312.5 --> 312 = 0x138

  121 00000000         ;UART0_C1

  123 00000000         ;0-->6:DOZEEN=doze enable (disabled)

  303 000000BC         ;>>>>> begin subroutine code <<<<<
  304 000000BC         GetHexIntMulti
                               PROC             {R0-R14}
  305 000000BC         ;Gets an n-word unsigned number from the user
  306 000000BC         ;typed in text hexadecimal representation,
  307 000000BC         ;and stores it in binary in memory
  308 000000BC         ; Input
  309 000000BC         ;  R0: Memory Address to store the Binary *Number
  310 000000BC         ;  R1: value of n(number of words in number) NumWords
  311 000000BC         ; Output
  312 000000BC         ;   C: 0 for Valid
  313 000000BC         ; Comments
  314 000000BC         ;     use 8n+1 as GetStringSB BufferCapacity: R1 
  315 000000BC         ;
  316 000000BC         ; psuedocode:
  317 000000BC         ;   1. convert buffer capacity into Bytes



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 10 Exercise 8 Multiprecision Arithemetic


  318 000000BC         ;  2. Store R0 somewehere else, for use by subroutines
  319 000000BC         ;  3. Store R0 with a Temp Varible, Perform GetStringSB on it
  320 000000BC         ;  4. Assume C Clear:
  321 000000BC         ;      LDRB from R0
  322 000000BC         ;      Clear R2
  323 000000BC         ;     Branch to a label -> Start Process
  324 000000BC         ;      LDRB from [R0.R2}
  325 000000BC         ;      check if number b/w 0x30 - 0x39
  326 000000BC         ;      subtract 0x30 from it, to extract the Decimal value.
  327 000000BC         ;
  328 000000BC         ;      check if number b/w 0x41 - 0x59 [A-Z] or 0x61 - 0x7A [a-z]
  329 000000BC         ;       read the input and change it to value.
  330 000000BC         ;      for hex 0x41 - 0x37 changes it to Decimal
  331 000000BC         ;        [A] - 55   = 10
  332 000000BC         ;        [a] - 0x57 = a 
  333 000000BC         ;      Store back to R0.R2
  334 000000BC         ;      R2++ 
  335 000000BC         ;      Compare R2 to R1
  336 000000BC         ;      if equal: pack
  337 000000BC         ;                       otherwise branch to above LDRB R0
  338 000000BC         ;
  339 000000BC         ;  packing:
  340 000000BC         ;    upCounter = 1
  341 000000BC         ; loop  offCounter = #bytes - 1 
  342 000000BC         ;       x = R0.offCounter
  343 000000BC         ;    y = R0.offCounter+1
  344 000000BC         ;    LSLS x,4 
  345 000000BC         ;    ADDS x,y
  346 000000BC         ;    STRB x,[result,upCounter]
  347 000000BC         ;    increment upCounter
  348 000000BC         ;    decrement offCounter by 2
  349 000000BC         ;    loop till end of string
  350 000000BC         
  351 000000BC B5FF            PUSH             {R0-R7, LR}
  352 000000BE         
  353 000000BE         ;convert buffer capacity into Bytes 
  354 000000BE         ;for use by GetStringSB
  355 000000BE 00C9            LSLS             R1, #3
  356 000000C0 1C49            ADDS             R1, R1, #1  ;R1 = 8n+1
  357 000000C2         
  358 000000C2         ;Store R0 in R7. R0 is used by other subroutines
  359 000000C2 0007            MOVS             R7, R0      ;R7 Mem Address of Number storage

  360 000000C4

  375 000000CE

  397 000000F2

  400 000000F6 428A            CMP              R2, R1      ;check if at end of input

  445 0000012A         ;----------------------------------------------------------------     
  446 0000012A         PutHexIntMulti
                               PROC             {R0-R14}
  447 0000012A         ; Outputs an n-word unsigned nummber 
  448 0000012A         ; Input 
  449 0000012A         ; R0: Memory address of unisgned n-word number
  450 0000012A         ;   R1: value of n(number of words in number)
  451 0000012A         ; Output
  452 0000012A         ; none
  453 0000012A         ;
  454 0000012A         ;pseudocode:
  455 0000012A         ; for (i=0, i < R1, i++){
  456 0000012A         ; PutNumHex(R0.(i));
  457 0000012A         ; }
  458 0000012A B507            PUSH             {R0-R2, LR}
  459 0000012C         
  460 0000012C 0002            MOVS             R2,R0       ;save the value of R0 to R2



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 14 Exercise 8 Multiprecision Arithemetic


  461 0000012E         ;PutNumHex takes input from R0
  462 0000012E         
  463 0000012E 0089            LSLS             R1,R1,#2    ;get the number of bytes   
  464 00000130 1F09            SUBS             R1,R1,#4    ;point to Most significant Word 
  465 00000132         
  466 00000132 5850    Loop    LDR              R0,[R2, R1]
  467 00000134 F7FF FFFE       BL               PutNumHex
  468 00000138         
  469 00000138 1F09            SUBS             R1,R1,#4    ;move back a word 
  470 0000013A D2FA            BHS              Loop
  471 0000013C         
  472 0000013C BD07            POP              {R0-R2, PC}
  473 0000013E                 ENDP
  474 0000013E         ;-----------------------------------------------------------------
  475 0000013E         
  476 0000013E         AddIntMultiU
                               PROC             {R1-R14}
  477 0000013E         ;Add the n-word unsigned number in register R2 to 
  478 0000013E         ;the n-word unsigned number in register R1. The result
  479 0000013E         ;is then stored in memory at address R0. The value located
  480 0000013E         ;in R3 is the number of words of each number that will be added.
  481 0000013E         ;C is then overwritten with either a 0 for success or the 
  482 0000013E         ;value of 1 for failure (overflow)
  483 0000013E         
  484 0000013E         ;Load in values one word (register) at a time
  485 0000013E         ;And add using ADCS to utilize the state of the ASPR c 
  486 0000013E         ;bit when carrying operations over.
  487 0000013E         
  488 0000013E         ;Inputs:
  489 0000013E         ;R1 = mem address of number 1 
  490 0000013E         ;R2 = mem address of number 2 
  491 0000013E         ;R3 = size of the numbers
  492 0000013E         ;Outputs
  493 0000013E         ;R0 = mem address to store result
  494 0000013E         ;C = Status value (0 for success and 1 for overflow)
  495 0000013E         ;-------------------------------------------
  496 0000013E         ; psuedocode
  497 0000013E         ; for (i=0; i< R3; i++){        ;for the enitre number
  498 0000013E         ; add1 = R1.[i];    ;load the next word value of number in R1 into variable
  499 0000013E         ; add2 = R2.[i];    ;load the next word value of number in R2 into variable
  500 0000013E         ; variable = add1 + add2;
  501 0000013E         ; }



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 15 Exercise 8 Multiprecision Arithemetic


  502 0000013E         ;
  503 0000013E         ; set first carry 0
  504 0000013E         ; preserve APSR  
  505 0000013E         ; 
  506 0000013E         ; loop:
  507 0000013E         ; MSR carry -> store it,  
  508 0000013E         ; word 1 + word2 + carry
  509 0000013E         ; preserve carry(MRS Carry) and STM R1!, {R3}
  510 0000013E         ; counter increment
  511 0000013E         
  512 0000013E         ;register retention
  513 0000013E B5FF            PUSH             {R0-R7, LR}
  514 00000140         
  515 00000140         ;Initalize state of C to 0
  516 00000140                 MOVC             #0          ;first carry in = 0
   56 00000140         ;------------------------------
   57 00000140         ;   Assign value to C PSR
   58 00000140         ;   To Set C  : MOVC #1
   59 00000140         ;   To Clear C: MOVC #0
   60 00000140         
   61 00000140 B401            PUSH             {R0}
   62 00000142 2000            MOVS             R0, #0
   63 00000144 0840            LSRS             R0, R0, #1
   64 00000146 BC01            POP              {R0}
   65 00000148         ;------------------------------ 
  517 00000148         
  518 00000148         ;preserve the PSR Flags
  519 00000148 F3EF 8700       MRS              R7, APSR
  520 0000014C         
  521 0000014C         ADD_WORD
  522 0000014C         ;check if at end of loop
  523 0000014C 2B00            CMP              R3, #0
  524 0000014E D009            BEQ              END_AddIntMultiU
  525 00000150         
  526 00000150         ;Since memory values are little endian,
  527 00000150         ;The least significant up to most significant
  528 00000150         ;Words can just be loaded into registers one by one.
  529 00000150 C920            LDM              R1!, {R5}
  530 00000152 CA40            LDM              R2!, {R6}
  531 00000154 F387 8800       MSR              APSR, R7
  532 00000158         
  533 00000158         ;word 1 + word2 + carry



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 16 Exercise 8 Multiprecision Arithemetic


  534 00000158 4175            ADCS             R5, R5, R6
  535 0000015A         
  536 0000015A         ;store addition in R0
  537 0000015A C020            STM              R0!, {R5}
  538 0000015C         ;store carry value
  539 0000015C F3EF 8700       MRS              R7, APSR
  540 00000160         
  541 00000160         ;Decrement word count
  542 00000160 1E5B            SUBS             R3, R3, #1
  543 00000162         
  544 00000162         ;Otherwise, just continue adding words
  545 00000162 E7F3            B                ADD_WORD
  546 00000164         
  547 00000164         END_AddIntMultiU
  548 00000164 F387 8800       MSR              APSR, R7
  549 00000168 BDFF            POP              {R0-R7, PC}
  550 0000016A                 ENDP

  650 000001EA         InitQueue
                               PROC             {R0-R14}
  651 000001EA         ;InitQueue: Initalize Circular FIFO Queue Structure
  652 000001EA         ;Inputs:
  653 000001EA         ; R0 - Memory location of queue buffer
  654 000001EA         ; R1 - Address to place Queue record structure
  655 000001EA         ; R2 - Size of queue structure (character capacity)

  657 000001EA         ; none

ARM Macro Assembler    Page 19 Exercise 8 Multiprecision Arithemetic


  659 000001EA B407            PUSH             {R0-R2}
  660 000001EC         
  661 000001EC         
  662 000001EC         ;Store memory address of front of queue
  663 000001EC         ;Into IN_PTR position of the buffer
  664 000001EC 6008            STR              R0, [R1, #IN_PTR]
  665 000001EE         
  666 000001EE         ;Store same memory address for OUT_PTR
  667 000001EE         ;position in the buffer since queue is empty
  668 000001EE 6048            STR              R0, [R1, #OUT_PTR]
  669 000001F0         
  670 000001F0         ;Store same memory address in BUF_STRT for initalization
  671 000001F0 6088            STR              R0, [R1, #BUF_STRT]
  672 000001F2         
  673 000001F2         ;Store BUF_PAST in last slot of buffer
  674 000001F2 1880            ADDS             R0, R0, R2
  675 000001F4 60C8            STR              R0, [R1, #BUF_PAST]
  676 000001F6         
  677 000001F6         ;Store BUF_SIZE with size in R2
  678 000001F6 740A            STRB             R2, [R1, #BUF_SIZE]
  679 000001F8

  681 000001F8         ;store in 6th slot of buffer
  682 000001F8 2000            MOVS             R0, #0
  683 000001FA 7448            STRB             R0, [R1, #NUM_ENQD]
  684 000001FC BC07            POP              {R0-R2}
  685 000001FE 4770            BX               LR
  686 00000200                 ENDP

  689 00000200         Dequeue PROC             {R1-R14}
  690 00000200         ;Dequeue: Remove an element from the circular FIFO Queue
  691 00000200         ;Inputs:

  693 00000200         ;Outputs:

  695 00000200         ; PSR C flag : Failure - C = 1

  700 00000202         ;If the number enqueued is 0,

  701 00000202         ;Set failure PSR flag

  703 00000204 2B00            CMP              R3, #0

  705 00000208         
  706 00000208 684C            LDR              R4, [R1, #OUT_PTR]
  707 0000020A

  715 0000020E 1E5B            SUBS             R3, R3, #1

  734 0000021E         ;Thus wrapping around the circular queue

 1006 00000340         GetChar PROC             {R1-R14}
 1007 00000340         ;/* Output:  R0:  Character received */
 1008 00000340         ; repeat 
 1009 00000340         ;      {check RDRF bit of UART0_S1
 1010 00000340         ;   }until (RDRF= 1)
 1011 00000340         ; get character received from UART0_D
 1012 00000340         ; return }
 1013 00000340 B40E            PUSH             {R1, R2, R3} ;Register retention
 1014 00000342         
 1015 00000342 4959            LDR              R1, =UART0_BASE
 1016 00000344 2208            MOVS             R2, #UART0_S1_OR_MASK
 1017 00000346 710A            STRB             R2, [R1,#UART0_S1_OFFSET]
 1018 00000348 2220            MOVS             R2, #UART0_S1_RDRF_MASK
 1019 0000034A         
 1020 0000034A         
 1021 0000034A         
 1022 0000034A 790B    repeat_get
                               LDRB             R3, [R1, #UART0_S1_OFFSET]
 1023 0000034C 4013            ANDS             R3, R3, R2
 1024 0000034E D0FC            BEQ              repeat_get
 1025 00000350         
 1026 00000350 79C8            LDRB             R0, [R1, #UART0_D_OFFSET] ;load value into R1 
 1027 00000352         
 1028 00000352 BC0E            POP              {R1, R2, R3} ;register retention
 1029 00000354         
 1030 00000354 4770            BX               LR          ;exit subroutine
 1031 00000356                 ENDP
 1032 00000356         



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 28 Exercise 8 Multiprecision Arithemetic


 1033 00000356         ;************************************************************************
 1034 00000356         PutChar PROC             {R0-R14}
 1035 00000356         ;/*Input: R0: Character to transmit */
 1036 00000356         ; repeat{
 1037 00000356         ;    check TDRE bit of UART0_S1
 1038 00000356         ; } until(TDRE == 1)
 1039 00000356         ; put character to transmit into UART0_D
 1040 00000356         ; return }
 1041 00000356         
 1042 00000356 B40E            PUSH             {R1, R2, R3} ;register retention 
 1043 00000358         
 1044 00000358 4953            LDR              R1, =UART0_BASE ;get value of TDRE
 1045 0000035A 2280            MOVS             R2, #UART0_S1_TDRE_MASK
 1046 0000035C         
 1047 0000035C         repeat_put
 1048 0000035C 790B            LDRB             R3, [R1, #UART0_S1_OFFSET]
 1049 0000035E 4013            ANDS             R3, R3, R2  ;check to see if ready for loading 
 1050 00000360 D0FC            BEQ              repeat_put  ;repeat unitl ready 
 1051 00000362         
 1052 00000362         
 1053 00000362 71C8            STRB             R0, [R1, #UART0_D_OFFSET] ;transmit characters from R0
 1054 00000364         
 1055 00000364         
 1056 00000364 BC0E            POP              {R1, R2, R3} ;register retention
 1057 00000366         
 1058 00000366 4770            BX               LR          ;exit subroutine
 1059 00000368         
 1060 00000368                 ENDP

 1116 000003A0         PutStringSB
                               PROC             {R0-R14}
 1117 000003A0         ;Prevents overrun of the buffer capacity, displays a null terminated string
 1118 000003A0         ; to the terminal screen

 1121 000003A0         ;R2 = Address of String Buffer
 1122 000003A0         
 1123 000003A0 B507            PUSH             {R0-R2, LR} ;register retention for nested subroutine
 1124 000003A2         
 1125 000003A2 2900            CMP              R1, #0      ;If all characters have been processed
 1126 000003A4 D009            BEQ              END_PutStringSB ;End subroutine execution

 1129 000003AA         READ_CHAR
 1130 000003AA 7810            LDRB             R0,[R2,#0]
 1131 000003AC 2800            CMP              R0,#NULL
 1132 000003AE D004            BEQ              END_PutStringSB

 1140 000003BA         
 1141 000003BA         END_PutStringSB

 1209 000003F6         DIVU    PROC             {R2-R14}
 1210 000003F6         ;****************************************************************
 1211 000003F6         ; Performs the division operation upon R1 by dividing it from R0
 1212 000003F6         ; and returning the Quotient and Remainder in R0 and R1 
 1213 000003F6         ; respectively. If Division by 0 is top be performed, R0 and R1 
 1214 000003F6         ; do not change their values, instead C bit is set.
 1215 000003F6         ;
 1216 000003F6         ; R0 rem R1 = R1 / R0 
 1217 000003F6         ;****************************************************************
 1218 000003F6 B40C            PUSH             {R2-R3}     ;Temporary Registers  
 1219 000003F8 2800            CMP              R0, #0      ;Check for division by 0
 1220 000003FA D014            BEQ              DIV_BY_0
 1221 000003FC 2900            CMP              R1, #0      ;Check for division of 0   
 1222 000003FE D00F            BEQ              DIV_OF_0
 1223 00000400         
 1224 00000400 0002            MOVS             R2, R0      ;Temporarily storing the dividend
 1225 00000402 2000            MOVS             R0, #0      ;Initializing the quotient
 1226 00000404         
 1227 00000404 4291    While   CMP              R1,R2       ;check for Dividend >= Divisor
 1228 00000406 D302            BLO              DIV_END
 1229 00000408 1A89            SUBS             R1,R1,R2    ;Dividend -= Divisor
 1230 0000040A 1C40            ADDS             R0,R0,#1    ;Quotient++
 1231 0000040C E7FA            B                While
 1232 0000040E         
 1233 0000040E F3EF 8200 
                       DIV_END MRS              R2, APSR    ;Clear flags.
 1234 00000412 2320            MOVS             R3, #C_MASK ;Create Mask
 1235 00000414 061B            LSLS             R3,R3,#C_SHIFT ;Shift to MSB
 1236 00000416 439A            BICS             R2,R3       ;
 1237 00000418 F382 8800       MSR              APSR, R2
 1238 0000041C         
 1239 0000041C BC0C    DIV_DONE



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 33 Exercise 8 Multiprecision Arithemetic


                               POP              {R2-R3}     ;Store Temporary Registers.
 1240 0000041E 4770            BX               LR
 1241 00000420         
 1242 00000420 2000    DIV_OF_0
                               MOVS             R0, #0      ;Set Quotient = 0
 1243 00000422 2100            MOVS             R1, #0      ;Set Remainder = 0
 1244 00000424 E7F3            B                DIV_END
 1245 00000426         
 1246 00000426 F3EF 8200 
                       DIV_BY_0
                               MRS              R2, APSR    ;Clear all flags
 1247 0000042A 2320            MOVS             R3, #C_MASK ;Mask
 1248 0000042C 061B            LSLS             R3,R3,#C_SHIFT
 1249 0000042E 431A            ORRS             R2,R3
 1250 00000430 F382 8800       MSR              APSR,R2     ;Set C Flag
 1251 00000434 E7F2            B                DIV_DONE
 1252 00000436                 ENDP
